    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-coursera---practical-machine-learning" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#coursera---practical-machine-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Coursera - Practical Machine Learning</h1>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-by-mandy-jiang--04042022" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#by-mandy-jiang--04042022"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>By Mandy Jiang  (04/04/2022)</h4>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-background-and-description" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#background-and-description"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Background and Description</h2>
<p dir="auto">The goal of this project is to use data from accelerometers on the belt, forearm, arm, and dumbell of 6 participants, to predict the manner in which they did the exercise. They were asked to perform barbell lifts correctly and incorrectly in 5 different ways. Variable "classe" in the training set shows which way they did in exercise, in which Class A corresponds to the specified execution of the exercise, while the other 4 classes correspond to common mistakes. (The Weight Lifting Exercise Datasethttp://web.archive.org/web/20161224072740/http:/groupware.les.inf.puc-rio.br/har)</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="library(ggplot2)
library(caret)
library(lattice)
library(e1071)
library(rpart)
library(kernlab)
library(randomForest)
library(gbm)"><pre>library(<span class="pl-smi">ggplot2</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">caret</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">lattice</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">e1071</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">rpart</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">kernlab</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">randomForest</span>)
library(<span class="pl-smi">gbm</span>)</pre></div>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-data-preprocessing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data-preprocessing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Data preprocessing</h2>
<p dir="auto">We are going to train and test the model on the training set only, and leave the testing set for final validation. Therefore, the data cleaning and preprocessin will be applied on training set only.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="train_file = 'https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/predmachlearn/pml-training.csv'
test_file = 'https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/predmachlearn/pml-testing.csv'
train = read.csv(train_file, sep=',', header=TRUE)
dim(train)
test = read.csv(test_file, sep=',', header=TRUE)
dim(test)"><pre><span class="pl-v">train_file</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/predmachlearn/pml-training.csv<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-v">test_file</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://d396qusza40orc.cloudfront.net/predmachlearn/pml-testing.csv<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-v">train</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> read.csv(<span class="pl-smi">train_file</span>, <span class="pl-v">sep</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>,<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">header</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">TRUE</span>)
dim(<span class="pl-smi">train</span>)
<span class="pl-v">test</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> read.csv(<span class="pl-smi">test_file</span>, <span class="pl-v">sep</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>,<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">header</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">TRUE</span>)
dim(<span class="pl-smi">test</span>)</pre></div>
<ol dir="auto">
	<li>19622</li>
	<li>160</li>

<ol dir="auto">
	<li>20</li>
	<li>160</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">We got 19622 observations and 160 variables in training dataset, while we got 20 observations and 160 variables in testing dataset. Next, we are going to remove variables with missing values and those not relevant to the prediction of classes in the training set.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="train = train[, colSums(is.na(train)) == 0]
train = train[,-c(1:7)]
dim(train)"><pre><span class="pl-v">train</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">train</span>[, colSums(is.na(<span class="pl-smi">train</span>)) <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>]
<span class="pl-v">train</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">train</span>[,<span class="pl-k">-</span>c(<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-c1">7</span>)]
dim(<span class="pl-smi">train</span>)</pre></div>
<ol dir="auto">
	<li>19622</li>
	<li>86</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Then we are going to remove variables with almost zero variance across observations.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="nvz = nearZeroVar(train)
train = train[,-nvz]
dim(train)"><pre><span class="pl-v">nvz</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> nearZeroVar(<span class="pl-smi">train</span>)
<span class="pl-v">train</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">train</span>[,<span class="pl-k">-</span><span class="pl-smi">nvz</span>]
dim(<span class="pl-smi">train</span>)</pre></div>
<ol dir="auto">
	<li>19622</li>
	<li>53</li>
</ol>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-data-splitting" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data-splitting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Data splitting</h2>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="set.seed(1886)
inTrain = createDataPartition(y=train$classe, p=0.7, list=FALSE)
training = train[inTrain,]

<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prediction-model-setup" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prediction-model-setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prediction model setup</h2>
<p dir="auto">We will use decision trees, random forests, Gradient Boosted Trees, and Support Vector Machine to predict the outcomes. We will also select the best performance model and look at the predictions on the testing dataset.</p>
<p dir="auto">Set up control for training with 5-fold cross validation.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="control = trainControl(method=&quot;cv&quot;, number=5, verboseIter=FALSE)"><pre><span class="pl-v">control</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> trainControl(<span class="pl-v">method</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cv<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>, <span class="pl-v">number</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-v">verboseIter</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">FALSE</span>)</pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-decision-tree" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#decision-tree"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Decision tree</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="modFit1 = train(classe~., data=training, method=&quot;rpart&quot;, trControl = control)

<div class="highlight highlight-source-r position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="AccuracyResults = data.frame(Model = c('Decision Tree','Random Forests','Gradient Boosted Trees',

                              Accuracy = rbind(cm1$overall[1],cm2$overall[1],cm3$overall[1],cm4$overall[1])
                             )
print(AccuracyResults)"><pre><span class="pl-v">AccuracyResults</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">data.frame</span>(<span class="pl-v">Model</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> c(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Decision Tree<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Random Forests<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Gradient Boosted Trees<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
                                        <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Support Vector Machine<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>),
                              <span class="pl-v">Accuracy</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> rbind(<span class="pl-smi">cm1</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">overall</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>],<span class="pl-smi">cm2</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">overall</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>],<span class="pl-smi">cm3</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">overall</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>],<span class="pl-smi">cm4</span><span class="pl-k">$</span><span class="pl-smi">overall</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>])
                             )
print(<span class="pl-smi">AccuracyResults</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                   Model  Accuracy
1          Decision Tree 0.4903993
2         Random Forests 0.9945624
3 Gradient Boosted Trees 0.9631266
4 Support Vector Machine 0.7816483"><pre><code>                   Model  Accuracy
1          Decision Tree 0.4903993
2         Random Forests 0.9945624
3 Gradient Boosted Trees 0.9631266
4 Support Vector Machine 0.7816483
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The best model is the Random Forest model, with 0.9945624 accuracy and therefore the out of sample error is 1-accuracy = 0.0054376, which is the smallest one across all 4 models.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prediction-on-test-set" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prediction-on-test-set"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Prediction on test set</h2>
